# Flower Delivery in New York City – Flordel Florist

We are a local **flower shop in New York City**, located in Manhattan’s Lower East Side (LES), dedicated to fast and reliable **flower delivery** throughout the city. Our primary focus is same-day **flower delivery in NYC**, with local service to Downtown Manhattan, Midtown, and Uptown (including Harlem and Washington Heights). We also deliver to Brooklyn, Queens, the Bronx, Staten Island, and select parts of New Jersey. [**Same-day delivery**](https://flordel.com/same-day-delivery.html "Same-day delivery") is available **7 days a week** for orders placed before **6:45 p.m.** We’re committed to handling every order with care and efficiency, ensuring your flowers arrive fresh and beautiful to your loved ones.

Whether it’s for a special occasion – a **birthday**, an **anniversary**, a **weekend brunch**, a **ceremony**, or _just because_ – we have the perfect fresh flowers and balloon arrangements for you. In addition to bouquets, we offer a variety of add-on gifts, including **balloons**, **teddy bears**, **candies**, and even **cakes** to make your surprise extra special. If you need to send **flowers in New York**, Flordel™ Florist is your top choice for quality, convenience, and unique designs. The easiest way to place an order is through [**Flordel.com**](https://flordel.com/ "Flordel.com"), and we also welcome orders by phone at **212-960-3542**.

## Your Lower East Side Manhattan Flower Shop (LES)

Our storefront is conveniently located at **78 Clinton St, New York, NY 10002** – ideal if you’re searching for a **flower shop near you** in Manhattan’s LES. We keep a wide variety of **fresh flowers** in stock, including popular blooms like **roses**, **lilies**, **peonies**, **tulips**, **sunflowers**, **orchids**, **hydrangeas**, **irises**, and more, as well as exotic tropical and seasonal flowers. We have **pre-made hand-tied bouquets** readily available for quick walk-ins in Downtown Manhattan. If you prefer something bespoke, our certified local florist (always on site) can create a **custom-made bouquet** just for you. We welcome walk-in customers and offer convenient curbside pickup from **7 a.m. to 7 p.m.** every day.

### NYC’s Highest-Rated Online Flower Delivery Service

We are proud to be one of the **highest-rated and most google-reviewed florists in New York City**. Known throughout the city as a **luxury florist**, we specialize in high-end, unique floral designs that delight New Yorkers and visitors alike. Since opening in 2019, our store has provided reliable same-day floral delivery, fulfilling over 60000 deliveries by 2025. Our team of certified designers is skilled in creating a wide range of flower arrangements – from elegant classic bouquets to modern, artistic compositions – to suit any occasion or style preference. We strive to use the freshest blooms and inventive designs, ensuring every arrangement feels special and one-of-a-kind.

Customer service is at the heart of Flordel. Our friendly support team is available from **7 a.m. to 7 p.m., seven days a week**, ready to assist you in **English or Spanish**. (Hablamos español.) If you have any custom requests or need guidance on the perfect arrangement, feel free to reach out – we’re happy to help make your gift unforgettable.

#### ❤️ Why Choose Flordel Florist?

- NYC boutique florist with a personal touch

- Same-day delivery every day

- Large selection of imported premium blooms

- Unique New York–style arrangements

- Loyal returning customers across all boroughs

- Fast, reliable, modern service

- Transparent prices & easy online checkout


##### ❓ FAQ — Flower Delivery in New York City

- Do you offer same-day delivery?

Yes. Same-day delivery is available 7 days a week for orders placed before 6:45 PM.

- Do you deliver to all NYC boroughs?

Yes — Manhattan, Brooklyn, Queens, Bronx, Staten Island, plus parts of New Jersey.

- Do you have peonies in winter?

Yes, we carry imported Chilean and Dutch peonies during off-season months.

- Can I request a custom bouquet?

Always — we specialize in made-to-order designs and custom color palettes.

- Where is your shop located?

Lower East Side, Manhattan, New York.

More [questions here.](https://flordel.com/faq "FAQ")

About Us

Flordel™ is a locally owned florist in NYC, proudly serving our community since 2019. We’ve grown to become the most Google-reviewed florist in New York, known for our unique floral designs and signature hand-tied bouquets that are beloved by both locals and visitors. We offer same-day flower delivery across all five boroughs of New York City (Manhattan, Brooklyn, Queens, the Bronx, and Staten Island) as well as parts of New Jersey. By 2024, we completed over 50,000 deliveries, a testament to the trust and support of our wonderful customers.

Our Lower East Side shop always has an impressive selection of flowers on hand – from seasonal and wildflowers to exotic tropical blooms. We source our flowers from around the world, including roses from Ecuador, orchids from Thailand, tulips from the Netherlands, and many more, to bring you the very best quality and variety. Every bouquet is crafted with care and a passion for floral artistry.

We love connecting with our customers and community. Follow our journey on Instagram, TikTok, and other social media platforms to see our latest arrangements and get inspired. When you think of flower delivery NYC, think Flordel Florist – we’re here to make every occasion bloom with beauty and joy.

# Garden roses

## Colombian Garden Roses in New York — Same-Day Delivery

Flordel's garden roses are sourced from **Colombian growers**, where the combination of high-altitude climate and year-round growing conditions produces blooms with exceptional petal density, natural fragrance, and the full cupped shape that defines the garden rose style. These are not the same as standard Ecuadorian roses: garden roses are a distinct botanical group — often including varieties like **Piano**, **Bombastic**, and **English roses** (in the David Austin tradition) — with a wider bloom head, many more petals per flower, and a softer, more romantic silhouette. A single garden rose head can be two to three times the diameter of a standard rose.

## Garden Roses vs. Standard Roses — The Key Differences

Buyers switching from standard roses to garden roses for the first time often describe the difference as immediately visible. Where a standard Ecuadorian rose has a tight, conical bloom with 20–30 petals, a garden rose opens into a shallow cup or rosette shape with 60–100+ petals, creating a denser, richer appearance. They also carry a natural scent that most hybrid tea roses bred for the commercial market have largely lost.

For buyers who want the full-bloom, soft-petal aesthetic of a [peony](https://flordel.com/flowers/peonies.html "Peonies NYC – Flordel") but in a rose — garden roses are the answer. Several arrangements in this collection, including the [Peony Roses Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/peony-roses-bouquet.html "Peony roses bouquet NYC – Flordel") and the [Piano Roses Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/piano-roses-bouquet.html "Piano roses bouquet NYC – Flordel"), are specifically chosen for their peony-like appearance. If you have been searching for roses that look like peonies in New York City, this is the collection.

## 15 Arrangements — What's in the Collection

The collection spans a range of presentation styles and rose varieties:

- **Boxed presentations** — [Large Garden Roses Box](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/large-garden-roses-box.html "Large garden roses box NYC – Flordel"), [Red Garden Roses Box](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/red-garden-roses-box.html "Red garden roses box NYC – Flordel"), and [Box of Garden Roses](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/box-of-garden-roses.html "Box of garden roses NYC – Flordel") — gift-ready formats where the full blooms are displayed flat or arranged in layers, showing the petal density to maximum effect.
- **Bouquets and bundles** — [Assorted Garden Rose Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/assorted-garden-rose-bouquet.html "Assorted garden rose bouquet NYC – Flordel"), [Garden Roses Bundle](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/garden-roses-bundle.html "Garden roses bundle NYC – Flordel"), [English Roses Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/english-roses-bouquet.html "English roses bouquet NYC – Flordel"), and [Peony Roses Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/peony-roses-bouquet.html "Peony roses bouquet NYC – Flordel").
- **Named-variety designs** — [Piano Roses Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/piano-roses-bouquet.html "Piano roses bouquet NYC – Flordel") (deep burgundy-pink tones, tightly cupped bloom) and [Basket of Bombastic Roses](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/basket-of-bombastic-roses.html "Basket of bombastic roses NYC – Flordel") (large pale blush blooms, especially popular for bridal and soft romantic arrangements).
- **Spray garden roses** — [Spray Garden Roses](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/giulia.html "Spray garden roses NYC – Flordel") and [Spray Garden Roses bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses/spray-garden-roses.html "Spray garden roses NYC – Flordel") — smaller-headed garden rose varieties that grow in clusters, adding texture and volume to mixed arrangements.

## Garden Roses for Weddings & Bridal Arrangements

Garden roses are among the most requested flowers for [wedding bouquets](https://flordel.com/wedding-bouquets.html "Wedding bouquets NYC – Flordel") and bridal party flowers in New York City, valued for their soft romantic shape, natural fragrance, and the way they photograph. They pair naturally with [peonies](https://flordel.com/flowers/peonies.html "Peonies NYC – Flordel"), [ranunculus](https://flordel.com/flowers/ranunculus.html "Ranunculus NYC – Flordel"), and [gypsophila](https://flordel.com/flowers/more-flowers/baby-s-breath-gypsophila.html "Baby's breath NYC – Flordel") in garden-style and free-form arrangements. For custom wedding or event orders, contact us directly at [212-960-3542](tel:+12129603542) or via [WhatsApp](https://wa.me/13479225921).

## Seasonality Note

Garden roses are available year-round from Colombian growers, though peak quality and the widest variety selection occur in spring and early summer. Winter availability is generally good but may be more limited for specific varieties. If you are planning a time-sensitive order for a specific named variety, confirming stock in advance is recommended.

## Same-Day Delivery Across New York City

Garden rose arrangements are available for same-day delivery across [Manhattan](https://flordel.com/manhattan-new-york-flower-delivery), [Brooklyn](https://flordel.com/brooklyn-new-york-flower-delivery), [Queens](https://flordel.com/queens-new-york-flower-delivery), [the Bronx](https://flordel.com/bronx-new-york-flower-delivery), [Upper West Side](https://flordel.com/upper-west-side-new-york-flower-delivery), [Midtown East](https://flordel.com/midtown-east-new-york-flower-delivery), [Financial District](https://flordel.com/financial-district-new-york-flower-delivery), [Gramercy](https://flordel.com/gramercy-new-york-flower-delivery), [NoMad](https://flordel.com/nomad-new-york-flower-delivery), [Kips Bay](https://flordel.com/kips-bay-new-york-flower-delivery) and more. # Red roses

## Red Roses Delivered Same Day Across New York City

Flordel carries 72 red rose arrangements — from a single dozen to 100 stems, from a simple wrapped bouquet to a boxed presentation or a mixed arrangement with baby's breath. All orders placed during business hours are available for same-day delivery across Manhattan, Brooklyn, Queens, and the Bronx. Every arrangement is prepared by hand at our [Lower East Side](https://flordel.com/lower-east-side-new-york-flower-delivery "Flower delivery Lower East Side NYC") studio using fresh Ecuadorian roses sourced for long stem length, full bloom stage, and deep color saturation.

## Find the Right Red Rose Arrangement

With 72 options available, here is how to navigate the collection by what matters most to you:

### By Stem Count

If the number of roses carries meaning — an anniversary year, a symbolic gesture, a milestone — start here. Flordel offers exact-count arrangements including a [dozen red roses](https://flordel.com/doce-rosas-rojas-elegantes.html "Dozen red roses NYC – Flordel") (the most requested count, carrying the symbolism of 12 months), as well as [50 red roses](https://flordel.com/roses/red-roses/50-red-roses.html "50 red roses NYC – Flordel"), [99 roses](https://flordel.com/roses/red-roses/99-roses.html "99 roses NYC – Flordel"), and [100 red roses](https://flordel.com/roses/red-roses/100-red-roses.html "100 red roses NYC – Flordel"). For a generous large-format bouquet without a fixed count, see the [Ramo Grande de Rosas Rojas](https://flordel.com/ramo-grande-de-rosas-rojas.html "Large red rose bouquet NYC – Flordel").

### By Presentation Style

Red roses at Flordel come in several distinct presentations. The [Ramo de Rosas Rojas Clásicas](https://flordel.com/ramo-de-rosas-rojas-clasicas.html "Classic red rose bouquet with baby's breath NYC – Flordel") pairs roses with [gypsophila (baby's breath)](https://flordel.com/flowers/more-flowers/baby-s-breath-gypsophila.html "Baby's breath NYC – Flordel") for the most traditional look. For a wrapped bouquet in craft paper, see [Red Roses with Brown Paper](https://flordel.com/roses/red-roses/red-roses-with-brown-paper.html "Red roses brown paper NYC – Flordel"). For a gift-ready box format, the [White Box of Red Roses](https://flordel.com/roses/red-roses/white-box-of-red-roses.html "White box of red roses NYC – Flordel") arrives display-ready with no additional prep.

### By Occasion and Message

Several arrangements are built around a specific intent rather than a presentation style. The [Ramo "Te Amo" de Rosas Rojas](https://flordel.com/ramo-te-amo-de-rosas-rojas.html "Ramo Te Amo NYC – Flordel") is designed for romantic declarations. The [Will You Marry Me Rose Bouquet](https://flordel.com/will-you-marry-me-rose-bouquet.html "Will You Marry Me rose bouquet NYC – Flordel") includes a proposal banner and is the only arrangement at Flordel designed exclusively for engagements. For anniversary gifts, see [Flores para Aniversario](https://flordel.com/roses/red-roses/flores-para-aniversario.html "Flores para Aniversario NYC – Flordel"). For a romantic first gesture, see [¿Quieres ser mi novia?](https://flordel.com/roses/red-roses/quieres-ser-mi-novia-2.html "¿Quieres ser mi novia? NYC – Flordel")

## About Our Red Roses

Flordel sources Ecuadorian red roses known for their exceptionally long stems — typically 50–70cm — and the density and depth of their bloom. Ecuadorian roses are grown at high altitude, which produces a slower, more compact development of the flower head and a longer vase life compared to roses grown at lower elevations. For customers who want a premium alternative to standard red roses, our [long stem roses](https://flordel.com/roses/long-stem-roses.html "Long stem roses NYC – Flordel") and [garden roses](https://flordel.com/roses/garden-roses.html "Garden roses NYC – Flordel") are sourced from Colombian growers and offer a different bloom shape and texture.

## Same-Day Red Rose Delivery Areas

We deliver red roses the same day to all five NYC boroughs and beyond. Key areas include [Manhattan](https://flordel.com/manhattan-new-york-flower-delivery), [Brooklyn](https://flordel.com/brooklyn-new-york-flower-delivery), [Queens](https://flordel.com/queens-new-york-flower-delivery), [the Bronx](https://flordel.com/bronx-new-york-flower-delivery), [Upper East Side](https://flordel.com/upper-east-side-new-york-flower-delivery), [Chelsea](https://flordel.com/chelsea-new-york-flower-delivery), [West Village](https://flordel.com/west-village-new-york-flower-delivery), [Tribeca](https://flordel.com/tribeca-new-york-flower-delivery), [Williamsburg](https://flordel.com/williamsburg-new-york-flower-delivery), [Park Slope](https://flordel.com/park-slope-new-york-flower-delivery), [Astoria](https://flordel.com/astoria-new-york-flower-delivery), [Long Island City](https://flordel.com/long-island-city-new-york-flower-delivery) and more. Full zone at [flordel.com/delivery →](https://flordel.com/delivery)

## Flordel Florist

Flordel Florist offers same-day flower delivery across Manhattan, Brooklyn, Queens, Bronx and Staten Island

# Blue roses

## Blue Roses in New York — How They're Made & What to Expect

True blue roses do not occur naturally. The blue rose arrangements in this collection are produced using premium Ecuadorian roses that have been color-enhanced — typically through dye absorption, where white or light-colored roses take up blue pigment through their stems — resulting in petals with a cool blue tone that holds through delivery. The depth and shade of blue can vary between arrangements and between batches, ranging from a soft periwinkle to a richer cobalt depending on the roses and the process used.

Because blue roses are not a standard stocked item at every wholesale supplier, **availability can vary**. We recommend confirming stock before placing your order by calling [212-960-3542](tel:+12129603542) or messaging via [WhatsApp](https://wa.me/13479225921). When available, many blue rose arrangements can be prepared for same-day or next-day delivery.

## 23 Blue Rose Arrangements — What's in the Collection

The collection spans two pages and covers a wide range of styles, from single-color blue bouquets to mixed designs that pair blue roses with complementary flowers:

- **Pure blue rose designs** — [Blue Roses Elegant Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/blue-roses-elegant-bouquet.html "Blue roses elegant bouquet NYC – Flordel"), [Blue Rose Bundle](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/blue-rose-bundle.html "Blue rose bundle NYC – Flordel"), [Large Blue Rose Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/large-blue-rose-bouquet.html "Large blue rose bouquet NYC – Flordel"), and [Hand Tied Blue Rose Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/hand-tied-blue-rose-bouquet.html "Hand tied blue rose bouquet NYC – Flordel") — for those who want blue roses to stand alone.
- **Boxed and basket presentations** — [Blue Rose Box](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/blue-rose-box.html "Blue rose box NYC – Flordel"), [Blue and White Rose Box](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/blue-and-white-rose-box.html "Blue and white rose box NYC – Flordel"), and [Blue Rose Basket](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/blue-rose-basket.html "Blue rose basket NYC – Flordel") — gift-ready formats that arrive display-ready.
- **Mixed-flower combinations** — [Blue Roses and](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/blue-roses-and-lisianthuses.html "Blue roses and lisianthus NYC – Flordel") [Lisianthus](https://flordel.com/flowers/lisianthus.html "Lisianthus NYC – Flordel"), [Blue Roses with Eucalyptus](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/blue-roses-with-eucalyptus.html "Blue roses with eucalyptus NYC – Flordel"), and [Sunflowers & Blue Roses](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/sunflowers-blue-roses-bouquet.html "Sunflowers and blue roses NYC – Flordel") — for those who want the cool tone of blue balanced by warmer or softer companion flowers.
- **Two-rose-color pairings** — [Red and Blue Roses Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses/red-and-blue-roses-bouquet.html "Red and blue roses bouquet NYC – Flordel") and the [Blue and Black Rose Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/blue-and-black-rose-bouquet.html "Blue and black rose bouquet NYC – Flordel") (in the black roses collection) — high-contrast combinations that make the blue pigment especially vivid.

## Blue Roses vs. Other Color-Enhanced Roses at Flordel

Blue roses belong to the same family of color-enhanced arrangements as [black roses](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses.html "Black roses NYC – Flordel") and [rainbow roses](https://flordel.com/roses/rainbow-roses.html "Rainbow roses NYC – Flordel") — all produced from naturally grown roses that have been altered to achieve colors not found in standard cultivation. The key differences:

- **Blue roses** — dye-absorbed through the stem; cool, elegant tone; availability varies by supplier stock.
- **[Black roses](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses.html)** — spray-painted; require advance notice; may have a faint paint odor.
- **[Rainbow roses](https://flordel.com/roses/rainbow-roses.html)** — multi-color dye absorption; vibrant and playful rather than cool or dramatic.

For a naturally grown rose in the blue-purple range, consider [purple roses](https://flordel.com/roses/purple-roses.html "Purple roses NYC – Flordel"), which are cultivated in deep lavender and plum tones without color enhancement.

## Occasions and Recipients

Blue roses are most often chosen for milestone [birthdays](https://flordel.com/happy-birthday.html "Birthday flowers NYC – Flordel") (particularly significant ones where an unexpected gift stands out), creative and corporate gifting, recipients who prefer cooler or more unusual aesthetics, and modern romantic gestures where red roses feel too conventional. Their rarity as a color-enhanced flower also makes them a natural choice for anyone who collects or appreciates visually distinctive objects.

## Delivery Across New York City

Once availability is confirmed, Flordel delivers blue roses to [Manhattan](https://flordel.com/manhattan-new-york-flower-delivery), [Brooklyn](https://flordel.com/brooklyn-new-york-flower-delivery), [Queens](https://flordel.com/queens-new-york-flower-delivery), [the Bronx](https://flordel.com/bronx-new-york-flower-delivery), [Woodside](https://flordel.com/woodside-new-york-flower-delivery), [Jackson Heights](https://flordel.com/jackson-heights-new-york-flower-delivery), [Forest Hills](https://flordel.com/forest-hills-new-york-flower-delivery), [Sunnyside](https://flordel.com/sunnyside-new-york-flower-delivery), [Riverdale](https://flordel.com/riverdale-new-york-flower-delivery), [Fort Greene](https://flordel.com/fort-greene-new-york-flower-delivery) and more. # Rose Delivery in New York City

## Premium Roses for Same-Day Flower Delivery in Manhattan and Nearby Areas

Roses remain one of the most requested flowers in New York because they fit almost every occasion — from anniversaries and birthdays to romantic surprises, apologies, luxury gifts, and elegant business deliveries. At Flordel, our rose collection includes premium red roses, white roses, pink roses, garden roses, and rare shades prepared daily for same-day delivery across Manhattan, Brooklyn, Queens, and nearby neighborhoods.

Many customers choosing roses also explore our [New York flower delivery](https://flordel.com/) collection when they want to combine roses with seasonal flowers such as [peonies](https://flordel.com/flowers/peonies.html), orchids, tulips, or hydrangeas for a fuller custom arrangement.

## Popular Rose Styles Ordered in New York

### Classic Red Roses for Romantic Gifts

Red roses remain the most popular choice for anniversaries, proposals, and romantic occasions. Customers often pair them with luxury wrapping or elegant presentation boxes.

[Explore Red Roses Collection](https://flordel.com/red-roses.html)

### Rare Rose Colors for Unique Floral Statements

Unusual rose shades continue growing in demand for customers looking for something more artistic, memorable, or visually unexpected.

[Blue Roses](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses.html) \| [Black Roses](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses.html)

### Luxury Roses with Seasonal Flowers

Premium rose bouquets are often combined with seasonal flowers for larger arrangements delivered to hotels, offices, and private residences across New York City.

[Peonies](https://flordel.com/flowers/peonies.html) \| [Orchids](https://flordel.com/orchids.html)

## Why Roses Stay the Strongest Floral Choice in NYC

Roses offer strong symbolism, long vase life, and visual flexibility. Whether you need a compact elegant bouquet or a large premium arrangement, roses remain one of the strongest options for same-day flower delivery in New York.

Customers ordering roses for Manhattan often also browse our [Manhattan flower delivery](https://flordel.com/manhattan-new-york-flower-delivery) page for local delivery options.

## Rose Delivery for Hotels, Offices, and Special Occasions

Roses are frequently delivered to hotels, office receptions, hospitals, and private apartments across New York City. Each arrangement is prepared daily to maintain freshness and presentation quality.

[Birthday Flowers](https://flordel.com/happy-birthday.html) \| [Romantic Flowers](https://flordel.com/romantic-flowers.html)

# Black roses

## Black Roses in New York — What You Need to Know Before Ordering

True black roses do not exist in nature. The arrangements in this collection are made by selecting premium Ecuadorian roses and applying a professional black spray paint to the petals. The result is a deep, matte black finish that holds its appearance through delivery. Because of the process involved, **black roses require advance notice and cannot be ordered for same-day delivery** — please contact us at [212-960-3542](tel:+12129603542) or via [WhatsApp](https://wa.me/13479225921) before placing your order to confirm availability and lead time.

One additional note: the spray-painting process can leave a faint paint odor on the roses. This typically dissipates within a few hours of delivery in a ventilated space. If the recipient has sensitivities to scent, this is worth considering when choosing your arrangement.

## 12 Black Rose Arrangements — What's in the Collection

Flordel's black rose collection spans several distinct presentation styles, each suited to different recipients and occasions:

- **Boxed presentations** — [Black Rose Round Box](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/black-rose-round-box.html "Black rose round box NYC – Flordel"), [Black Roses Heart Box](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/black-roses-heart-box.html "Black roses heart box NYC – Flordel"), and the [Black Box](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/black-box.html "Black box roses NYC – Flordel") — gift-ready formats that arrive display-ready with no additional prep.
- **Two-color combinations** — [Red and Black Rose Box](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/red-and-black-rose-box.html "Red and black rose box NYC – Flordel"), [Black and White Roses](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/black-and-white-roses.html "Black and white roses NYC – Flordel"), [Black and White Roses Heart](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/black-and-white-roses-heart.html "Black and white roses heart NYC – Flordel"), [Blue and Black Rose Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/blue-and-black-rose-bouquet.html "Blue and black rose bouquet NYC – Flordel"), and [Black Roses and Sunflowers](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/black-roses-and-sunflowers.html "Black roses and sunflowers NYC – Flordel") — for those who want the drama of black roses softened or contrasted by a second color.
- **Sculptural / conceptual designs** — [Yin Yang](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/yin-yang.html "Yin Yang rose arrangement NYC – Flordel") (black and white roses arranged in the yin-yang symbol) and the [heart-shaped arrangement](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/black-and-white-roses-heart.html "Black and white roses heart NYC – Flordel") — design-forward pieces for gifting that goes beyond a standard bouquet.
- **Volume arrangements** — [100 Black Roses](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/100-black-roses.html "100 black roses NYC – Flordel") and the [Black Roses Bouquet](https://flordel.com/roses/black-roses/black-roses-bouquet.html "Black roses bouquet NYC – Flordel") — for statement deliveries where scale reinforces the impact.

## Who Orders Black Roses — and Why

Black roses are most frequently requested for occasions where conventional flowers would feel out of place: **Halloween** arrangements, [gifts for him](https://flordel.com/occasions/for-him.html "Flowers for him NYC – Flordel") who prefers unconventional aesthetics, fashion or editorial events, gallery openings, theatrical performances, and recipients who have an affinity for dark or gothic visual styles. They are also chosen as a bold romantic gesture by those who find red roses predictable — the statement is the same, but the register is entirely different.

For a similar dramatic palette with a naturally grown flower, consider [blue roses](https://flordel.com/roses/blue-roses.html "Blue roses NYC – Flordel") (also color-enhanced, in a cooler dark tone) or [purple roses](https://flordel.com/roses/purple-roses.html "Purple roses NYC – Flordel") (naturally available in deep jewel tones). For classic contrast alongside black roses, [white roses](https://flordel.com/roses/white-roses-1.html "White roses NYC – Flordel") are the most striking pairing.

## How to Order Black Roses in NYC

Because black roses require spray-painting and drying time, they cannot be prepared for immediate same-day dispatch. To place an order:

- Call [212-960-3542](tel:+12129603542) or message via [WhatsApp +1 347-922-5921](https://wa.me/13479225921) to confirm lead time and availability.
- Let us know your preferred arrangement, stem count, and delivery date and address.
- Once confirmed, you can complete your order online or over the phone.

Flordel delivers black roses across [Manhattan](https://flordel.com/manhattan-new-york-flower-delivery), [Brooklyn](https://flordel.com/brooklyn-new-york-flower-delivery), [Queens](https://flordel.com/queens-new-york-flower-delivery), [the Bronx](https://flordel.com/bronx-new-york-flower-delivery), [Staten Island](https://flordel.com/staten-island-new-york-flower-delivery), [Greenpoint](https://flordel.com/greenpoint-new-york-flower-delivery), [DUMBO](https://flordel.com/dumbo-new-york-flower-delivery), [Carroll Gardens](https://flordel.com/carroll-gardens-new-york-flower-delivery), [Red Hook](https://flordel.com/red-hook-new-york-flower-delivery), [Elmhurst](https://flordel.com/elmhurst-new-york-flower-delivery) and more. Full delivery zone at [flordel.com/delivery →](https://flordel.com/delivery)

## Also in the Roses Collection

# Spring Flowers

Spring Flowers - Gift Guide - Flordel

# Spring Flowers

Awakening and possibility. Spring flowers celebrate renewal, natural abundance, and the profound hope that comes when the world returns to life. These are flowers for moments of beginning, for acknowledging growth, and for recognizing that sometimes the greatest gift is simply witnessing what emerges when conditions become right.

Spring changes everything. The world awakens, light returns, and new growth becomes visible. Spring flowers capture this energy—they are fresh, they are full of possibility, and they suggest that beginning again is not just possible but natural. There is something deeply hopeful about spring flowers. They do not apologize for being new. They celebrate emergence, growth, and the understanding that renewal is always available to us.

* * *

## For New Beginnings and Fresh Starts

Life chapters beginning with genuine hope. New homes and fresh spaces. Transitions embraced with optimism. Celebrations of people starting over with courage. Encouragement for those taking brave new steps. Recovery marked with the understanding that spring follows every winter. Any moment when new beginning feels like genuine possibility rather than frightening change.

### Spring Selection

Choose [fresh, contemporary selections](https://flordel.com/green-hydrangea-bouquet.html) that feel new and hopeful. Or select [arrangements celebrating inner strength and clarity](https://flordel.com/yellow-irises-bouquet.html). Both capture spring's promise of genuine beginning and fresh perspective.

* * *

## For Celebrating Growth and Renewal

Recognition of people moving through personal growth. Acknowledgment of transformation and positive change. Celebration of spring itself and the renewal it represents. Moments when you want to mark that something beautiful is emerging. Thank you gifts for those who have supported your growth. Any occasion honoring the courage required for genuine renewal.

### Growth Recognition

Consider [selections expressing pure happiness and straightforward joy](https://flordel.com/sunflowers-yellow-roses-bouquet.html). Or choose [arrangements with honest, garden-fresh beauty](https://flordel.com/assorted-scabiosa-bouquet.html). Both celebrate growth without fanfare and renewal with genuine warmth.

* * *

## For Expressing Hope and Possibility

Encouragement for those navigating uncertain times. Expressions of belief in someone's potential. Moments when you want to say I see your possibility, I believe in what you are becoming. Celebrations of optimism grounded in genuine springtime energy. Recognition that sometimes the most meaningful gift is simply witnessing and affirming what someone is becoming.

### Hope and Optimism

Select [arrangements celebrating personality and authentic character](https://flordel.com/sunflowers-snapdragons-bouquet.html). Or choose [selections offering uncomplicated joy and straightforward warmth](https://flordel.com/zinnias-bouquet.html). Both communicate genuine hope and belief in possibility.

* * *

## For Spring Celebrations and Gatherings

Spring invites gathering. Garden celebrations, outdoor moments, and the simple joy of being outside together. Spring flowers work beautifully for spaces where natural light and natural elements already create beauty. Choose arrangements that enhance rather than compete with the season itself.

### Spring Gatherings

Choose [vibrant, celebratory selections](https://flordel.com/collections/celebration-flowers) that feel appropriate to outdoor spaces. Or select [arrangements capturing the ease and brightness of warm seasons](https://flordel.com/summer-flowers-guide.html). Both work beautifully for spring moments of gathering and joy.

* * *

## Seasonal Timing

**Spring availability:** Peak season for fresh, locally-inspired selections. **Easter and spring holidays:** Plan ahead during peak spring holiday weeks. **Spring weather:** Consider placement carefully—outdoor flowers benefit from protected areas during unpredictable spring weather. **Delivery:** Same-day delivery available throughout New York City during spring season.

* * *

# Same day delivery

- **We take same-day delivery orders until 6:00 pm** as  the latest. Don't wait till the last minute. Based on the shipping address and the time you placed an order, we may not confirm the order.
- **We are open today.** 7 days a week (inc Saturday and Sunday)/all holidays without exceptions.
- Delivery **takes 2 hours and up** depending on the delivery address and the product you choose.
- If you want us to deliver your order ASAP, please place an order on the website ASAP.
- All products from the same-day delivery page are available for your order today. We can guarantee today's delivery only for same-day delivery page products. If you want to check the availability of other bouquets, feel free to contact us.

# Same-Day Flower Delivery in New York City

Flordel offers **same-day flower delivery in New York City** for customers who need fresh flowers delivered quickly, professionally, and with reliable timing. Orders placed before the daily cut-off are prepared immediately by our florists and delivered across **Manhattan, Brooklyn, Queens, the Bronx, Staten island, and nearby areas**. Our same-day collection includes roses, peonies, orchids, lilies, flower boxes, balloons, plants, and premium gift sets available for fast local delivery. Orders paid before **6:00 PM** qualify for same-day service, with most deliveries completed within **2–3 hours depending on address and product availability**.

## Same-Day Roses, Bouquets, Orchids, and Gift Sets in NYC

Customers searching for **same-day flower delivery NYC**, **flowers delivered today Manhattan**, **urgent florist near me**, or **last-minute roses New York** often choose [Flordel](http://flordel.com/ "Flower delivery New York") because the shop offers both classic bouquets and premium custom floral designs prepared fresh daily. Popular same-day products include red roses, mixed seasonal bouquets, orchids in pots, rose boxes, teddy bears, balloons, and luxury arrangements suitable for birthdays, anniversaries, romantic surprises, sympathy flowers, and business deliveries.

## Fast Local Flower Delivery with Flexible Coverage

Flordel delivers throughout New York with local pricing by zone, including **$9 delivery across most Manhattan neighborhoods**, plus service to Brooklyn, Queens, the Bronx, and selected New Jersey areas. Orders are usually confirmed within **15 minutes**, and customers can also request next-day delivery, scheduled delivery, or premium timed delivery when needed. Specific-time delivery is available with additional service options.

## Why Same-Day Flower Delivery Performs Strongly in NYC

Same-day flower orders remain one of the highest-converting floral searches because many customers buy flowers for urgent occasions: forgotten birthdays, last-minute apologies, surprise gifts, hospital visits, and same-evening celebrations. Fast local delivery combined with premium presentation is one of the strongest trust signals for flower buyers in New York
